1490402641280< /date>
< Rating>

< Text>
This is the first time Ive written a review. My experience was so terrible that I felt obligated to do so. When I went into the shop I was immediately greeted with a smile. I asked the gentlemen in the first chair how many people are waiting. Visibly there were 3 however he told me that I'd be next because 1 was waiting for another barber not yet in and the other two were hanging out I guess. So I said cool and paid the meter and took a seat. There were 4 out 5 barbers and right before a chair was available an older gentleman walked in. And as soon as the chair became available the barber immediately asked him tp take a seat. I am a very patient person so I decided not to say anything halfway assuming maybe he had an appointment. (making excuses for them, I guess). So now about a 45 minutes had gone by, a long time for being next. Then the barber in the first chair was done so of course I assumed that he'd be the one to cut me next. Nope! He grabbed one of the guys that was sitting there before I walked in. After he had said the he didn't want a cut! So, ok he changed his mind, I can't get upset after all he WAS there before I. So now I have been there for a little over an hour. Finally the barber directly in front is finished, by then there isn't anyone else waiting but me. The 5th chair barber gets in and grabs the last guy waiting before I. Clearly Im next. NOPE! The barber disappears to the back and 10 minutes later emerges with basket full of towels. Now I am sitting there, looking at an open chair, watching the only available barber fold towels, like he works for bed, bath and beyond and not a barbershop. By now things are extremely awkward because no one has said anything to me since I first walked in, in fact no one even acknowledged that I was there. I guess they assumed that I just wanted to watch them cut other peoples hair and talk about there trip to Vegas. Then Finally after about an hour and a half, the first and only guy that had spoke to me and asked the most obvious question "Are you still waiting?" I said yes of course then he gets the towel folding barber and asks him to cut my hair. SMDH! I was directly in front of the guy the whole time. I finally get in the chair and the barber had zero conversation, actually it seemed as though he hated his job and would much rather be folding towels than cutting my hair. I should've risked it but I did. I have to say it was the most awkwardly silent 30 minutes of my hair cut life. I am 35 and have been getting a hair cut all over the country every other week since I was 5. Honestly this fade was subpar to even supercuts or great clips. I wouldn't recommend this shop to even a homeless person, even if the cut was free. I wish they had a 303 Barbershop out here. Always top of the line fades and not once have I been disappointed.< /Text>

<Time>1616684565497<//Time><Rate>1</Rate>< review>
Stay away from this shady local rental car company. My rental car was merely driven 65 miles when I parked it at my hotel in Menifee, CA. The rental car remained parked overnight, and when I got in to drive to San Diego the dashboard signaled with a low tire pressure indicator. I step out and the tire is flat to the ground. I had to change the tire myself since I declined their coverage and they wouldn't send roadside assistance (fine).

I get back to return the rental car and I'm told I have to file an incident report because of the flat tire (no foreign objects were found that would have punctured the tire). The rental car would be taken to a service center so they can determine if the tire can be patched or it has to be replaced altogether. According to them, the rental car was given to me in good condition and I'm returning it with a flat tire...what assurances do I get the company has properly done maintenance on the tires???

A few days I get a call from Fernando (Accounting) telling me I owe them $100 for the tire. He gives me no explanation as to why the tire needed to be replaced and why it can't be patched. I tell him I'd pay as long as a valid reason is given to me. He can't give me a reason because the service center didn't put one in the paperwork even though they "thoroughly investigated it".

I call my personal insurance so they can find out what happened but they're unable to get a hold of Fernando and they leave 2 voicemails. I then receive an email from a third-party claims company and now I'm due $150 which will go to collections if not fully paid which will impact my credit score.

Rental Car Cafe and its business practices need to be called out because they're clearly not willing to work with their customers and ultimately make the rental experience a nightmare. I will never rent from them again, and though their rates may be low, I encourage you to stay away from them (pay the extra money and go to an established and trusted rental car company).<//review>

Stay away from this horrible local rental car company. My rental car was merely driven 65 miles when I parked it at my hotel in Menifee, CA. The rental car remained parked overnight, and when I got in to drive to San Diego the dashboard signaled with a low tire pressure indicator. I step out and the tire is flat to the ground. I had to change the tire myself since I declined their coverage and they wouldn't send roadside assistance (fine).

I get back to return the rental car and I'm told I have to file an incident report because of the flat tire (no foreign objects were found that would have punctured the tire). The rental car would be taken to a service center so they can determine if the tire can be patched or it has to be replaced altogether. According to them, the rental car was given to me in good condition and I'm returning it with a flat tire...what assurances do I get the company has properly done maintenance on the tires???

A few days I get a call from Fernando (Accounting) telling me I owe them $100 for the tire. He gives me no explanation as to why the tire needed to be replaced and why it can't be patched. I tell him I'd pay as long as a valid reason is given to me. He can't give me a reason because the car service center didn't put one in the paperwork even though they "thoroughly investigated it".

I call my personal insurance so they can find out what happened but they're unable to get a hold of Fernando and they leave 2 voicemails. I then receive an email from a third-party claims company and now I'm due $150 which will go to collections if not fully paid which will impact my credit score.

Update: I was able to obtain the estimate report from the car service center (Evans Tire & Service Centers) through the third-party claims company and I was able to call them. After providing some information, they confirmed the following: 1) they didn't inspect or even look at the tire 2) Justin (Owner of Car Rental Cafe) personally knows the manager of the car service center for years and had called him from his personal mobile phone to tell him to go ahead and outright replace the tire. Of course, I follow up with Fernando and he basically washes his hands and even goes as far to tell me I was at fault because I was given the opportunity to settle with them on the side and now things were out of their hands and can't do anything to help and implies I'm making this up.

Car Rental Cafe and its shameless and shady business practices need to be called out because they're clearly not willing to work with their customers and ultimately make the rental experience a nightmare. I will never rent from them again, and though their rates may be low, I encourage you to stay away from them as far away as possible (pay the extra money and go to an established and trusted rental car company). Car Rental Cafe will take advantage of you as a renter, and stiff you with a bill that's is unfounded because they engage in this kind of deplorable methods.<//review>

We called them, and they told us to come back in and we can give them the ticket and they will pay for it. They informed us not to worry about being charged for the ticket. So we turned around from where we were going and drove 35 minutes back to the car rental shop to give them the ticket and get a temporary registration for the car. By this time the guy we talked to over the phone wasn't working anymore, he was done for the day and he didn't leave any notes like he said he would. So we had to re explain the whole situation to someone new. That employee said they would leave a note saying that they are comping us gas for our whole honeymoon. When we took the car back that note wasn't there either, and once again we were talking to someone new who we had to explain the whole situation to again.  luckily we didn't have to pay for any of the gas. Once again they informed us not to worry about the ticket and that they will pay for it. A month has gone by and we received a letter in the mail stating that we were charged for the ticket, and a $50 service fee. We called Travcar, talked with someone new, had to explain the whole situation again because no one left any notes or had any kind of documentation about the ticket, and we were told that the citation company who sent us the letter isn't a company they do business with. They gave us the number to call and it was the exact same number as what was on the letter we received. They don't even know who they do business with. <text>The low prices are not worth the hassle here. Always check exactly what you're being charged for and read your receipts carefully, or you might get overcharged without you knowing! Thank God I was at least somewhat warned about this, so here I am passing on that warning (confirmed by my own experience) to you all. Initially I booked them for 4 days because they were the cheapest car rental I could find. I was moving cross country and waiting for my car to arrive, and so I only needed a rental car for a little over a week before mine would arrive. On Priceline I paid around $48 for an economy car. I get there, exhausted after about 12 hours of flying (and yes, two shuttles from the airport, as mentioned by another reviewer, the second of which they never called to let me know they arrived, leaving me waiting for about 10-15 mins in drizzling rain with many suitcases). I tell them I don't want any of their insurance, I will use my own, and I will fill up the gas on my own (no additional charges, in other words). The guy then says, "Okay your car is going to take a few more minutes to get ready, but we have a few Hyundai's ready for you now, midsize cars" (i.e. an upgrade). I tell him it's okay, I'll wait. My car arrives, it's a blue Nissan Sentra, and I complete the paperwork and drive off (and I found out later I was supposed to get a receipt and the rental agreement, didn't get either).

The next day I decide to just extend my 4 day rental to 11 days, and call Travcar/Ace to do so. The guy reads out the charges to me, "So it'll be $73 for your initial 4 days..." And I'm like WHAT?!? I paid $48, not $73! And he goes, "No, you agreed to a midsize vehicle, I see it right here". We start arguing, he says he can't refund the difference nor remove it from the next reservation I'm about to make without tacking on an additional $10/day for extending the rental. I decide to return the midsize vehicle I have and cease all business with them. I cancel my apartment hunting plans and drive over there furious. The guy realizes I never got a receipt, so I didn't know what I was being charged for, and lets me keep the midsize for economy price, and says I won't be charged the $73 (it was still pending at that point when I checked my banking app, so I believed they would change it). That was nice of him.

Based on that goodwill and because it was simply more convenient for me, plus the price being low relative to other vendors, I place a new reservation for an economy car for the remaining 7 days I'd need a car. It comes out to about $125 on Priceline (so total, $48 + $125 = $173). I go to swap my midsize car for an economy. The guy, knowing all my previous history, says that he can let me keep this midsize car for even cheaper than the economy car. The difference from last time would also be rolled in to that charge. Ultimately I am charged $173, which isn't cheaper than what I had originally, but oh well, I got to keep my car for economy prices.

TL;DR Book with caution here. Make sure you get a receipt and read your receipts very carefully to make sure you're getting charged only for what you paid for, nothing more.<//text>< Gmap_id>

I also requested an invoice/receipt for the payment as my company needs this for tax and expense purposes.

Do you thing that the imbecile's at TravCar have had the courtesy of responding.....nothing, nil, nada, nich, nulla........SAD!!

Looking at the other reviews on TravCar (on Yelp! for instance) there is only one thing that I can suggest- RENT ELSEWHERE!!!!!!!</Text>

< text>
Just spent 4 days there. Great beach (although it was cold) Campgrounds were decent. We were in spot 64, which was between the highway and the beach. Heard more of the highway traffic at night,but if wasn't distracting. Showers have warm water which is why I gave 5 stars. Showers cost 25 cent for about 3 minutes.
Word of caution, the last night I thought I heard a familiar noise around 4am....sure enough the next morning my suspicion was right. Racoons got into and ripped our trash bag which was hanging on a line....so be careful....they have those little critters around the campgrounds. If ya can reserve a lot closer to the beach (79 thru 87).</text>

<Rating>5< /Rating><response>None<//response><review>When traveling along the California Coast on the 101 near Santa Barbara, you simply must stop at El Capitan State Beach, even if only for a short while.  There is a $10 day use fee here, which is money well spent.  You'll experience a short, picturesque nature trail to a gorgeous beach.  Eye-pleasing greenery was everywhere when we visited in January.  We saw one jaw-droppingly massive tree surrounded by a bed of nasturtium, which stands out on this lovely trail. We also saw a fat Red-Shouldered Hawk, sunning itself in a tree on our hike, along with stunning beach views.</review>< Time>

<username>M. Gonnerman</username><time>1575481343782</time><rate>5</rate>< text>
The most beautiful, best campground in the world in this reviewers opinion. Feel like you are in the mountains as you camp, then stroll down to the beach and walk along sandstone cliffs and the mostly calm ocean with the Channel Islands in sight. Birds, seals and other nature abound, so please keep dogs at the campsite and off the beach. The camp store is open all year. Please patronize it, as that keeps it going! Don‚Äôt forget your quarters for the showers (two minutes for 25cents what a deal!). Side note: be aware during fire season, conditions change quickly.</text>

< review>
One of my favorite local ‚Äúbeach‚Äù campgrounds. So many great tent camping sites with ocean views and nature walks nearby. The trails are great and most are dog friendly, shaded, and peaceful (except for the actual beach/sand... no dogs allowed). The beach itself is pretty with gorgeous rock formations at the far end- definitely worth the walk. The nature trails too run along a creek and are so lush, tranquil, and serene.

Depending on what you‚Äôre looking for, if you‚Äôre coming for camping, here are my suggestions for campsites: ‚Ä¢Very shaded and private, near cost but not visible- more about trees and nature #99, Partial sea views and trees/privacy #101, Best and Fullest ocean views but more open/no shade #105-107, Complete nature cove of green and private, nearby access to ocean and trails #41.</review>

< Text>
It's a gun shop..not a thrift store or a hardware store.. GUNS and ammo (if you buy a gun). I understand both the angst from customers and from the shop owners. These are sketchier times. As far as my runnings with the shop.. generally prickly at times and warmer customer service at other times.. just depends on the moment.  I have had excellent suggestions and have not been led astray for the sake of a sale. When something wasn't right about a purchase they took extra effort and even did some tactical repair work to make things right. I go back when the occasion arises. We don't have many options in San Francisco so just call before you go and get things clear about your intentions with the shop. My 3 cents...</Text>

This spot was one of the few local coffee shops that was open Labor Day morning in the area so gave it a shot. The woman who worked there was very sweet and clarified my order when I placed it and when she handed it to me. The breakfast sandwiches were huge and worth it in my opinion price wise.

<name>Fuse Henry< /name><Time>1617981849103< /Time>< Rate>
1< /Rate>
< text>
Most of the food at Thai Stars is ok. We've ordered from them on several occasions, but there has always been at least two items that didn't live up to the quality we expected. As of our most recent meal, we've decided that we're done with them.

The Pad See Ew is pretty good, and the currys are pretty good.  Avoid the Orange Chicken and Sweet & Sour Chicken, as they're poor quality and not worth the price.

We've only kept ordering from them because often, they're the only Thai place that's open for delivery, but from now on, if no other Thai place is available, then we're just just not having Thai food.

One of the items we ordered on our last order (yesterday) was the Red Curry. On all other occasions, the curry was in a good sized container, but this time, it's like the order was halved. We did not order a lunch portion or anything like that. In fact, DoorDash lets you know the date of the last time you ordered a certain item, and I simply re-ordered the same Red Curry as about a month ago. Same item, same price, much smaller portion.

I don't know if they ran out of ingredients or what, but why should I pay the same amount for such a small portion?  If they had to significantly reduce the portion size for some reason, it should be noted on the menu.  We also special ordered it to be "Not Spicy" (Expecting at least less spicy).  The spiciness of Red Curry can easily be controlled, but they sent us the HOTTEST Red Curry I've ever tasted in my entire life. My wife gagged on just a teaspoon full, then I tried it and was pretty shocked at the heat level.  Based on other experiences with this restaurant, we think that maybe they didn't like us asking for the Red Curry to be "Not Spicy" (We know it will be anyway, but we wanted it as mild as possible) so they responded by making it as hot as possible.  We added TWO CANS of Coconut Milk to the Red Curry which made it edible, but it was still very, very hot.  We had to take hardcore antacids to eat a portion.

We won't be back.<//text>

Went in earlier this evening to order take out and it was pleasantly unbusy.
Placed and paid for my 4-meal order and in reasonable course was brought two nicely full bags.

I've been coming here for a long time now. My family and I usually make late night trips here after a long day. They are always friendly and most of the staff knows us. The service is always great and the food is good too. We have never had a problem here in all the time we've been going there.
